         log.trace(\\\"Allocating a new {} byte message buffer for topic {} partition {} with remaining timeout {}ms\\\", size, topic, effectivePartition, maxTimeToBlock);\\n332:                     // This call may block if we exhausted buffer space.\\n333:                     buffer = free.allocate(size, maxTimeToBlock);\\n334:                     // Update the current time in case the buffer allocation blocked above.\\n335:                     // NOTE: getting time may be expensive, so calling it under a lock\\n336:                     // should be avoided.\\n337:                     nowMs = time.milliseconds();\\n338:                 }\\n339: \\n340:                 synchronized (dq) {\\n341:                     // After taking the lock, validate that the partition hasn't changed and retry.\\n342:                     if (partitionChanged(topic, topicInfo, partitionInfo, dq, nowMs, cluster))\\n343:                         continue;\\n344: \\n345:                     RecordAppendResult appendResult = appendNewBatch(topic, effectivePartition, dq, timestamp, key, value, headers, callbacks, buffer, nowMs);\\n346:                     // Set buffer to null, so that deallocate doesn't return it back to free pool, since it's used in the batch.\\n347:                     if (appendResult.newBatchCreated)\\n348:                         buffer = null;\\n349:                     // If queue has incomplete batches we disable switch (see comments in updatePartitionInfo).\\n350:                     boolean enableSwitch = allBatchesFull(dq);\\n351:                     topicInfo.builtInPartitioner.updatePartitionInfo(partitionInfo, appendResult.appendedBytes, cluster, enableSwitch);\\n352:                     return appendResult;\\n353:                 }\\n354:             }\\n355:         } finally {\\n356:             free.deallocate(buffer);\\n357:             appendsInProgress.decrementAndGet();\\n358:         }\\n359:     }\\n360: \\n361:     /**\\n362:      * Append a new batch to the queue\\n363:      *\\n364:      * @param topic The topic\\n365:      * @param partition The partition (cannot be RecordMetadata.UNKNOWN_PARTITION)\\n366:      * @param dq The queue\\n367:      * @param timestamp The timestamp of the record\\n368:      * @param key The key for the record\\n369:      * @param value The value for the record\\n370:      * @param headers the Headers for the record\\n371:      * @param callbacks The callbacks to execute\\n372:      * @param buffer The buffer for the new batch\\n373:      * @param nowMs The current time, in milliseconds\\n374:      */\\n375:     private RecordAppendResult appendNewBatch(String topic,\\n376:                                               int partition,\\n377:                                               Deque<ProducerBatch> dq,\\n378:                                               long timestamp,\\n379:                                               byte[] key,\\n380:                                               byte[] value,\\n381:                                               Header[] headers,\\n382:                                               AppendCallbacks callbacks,\\n383:                                               ByteBuffer buffer,\\n384:                                               long nowMs) {\\n385:         assert partition != RecordMetadata.UNKNOWN_PARTITION;\\n386: \\n387:         RecordAppendResult appendResult = tryAppend(timestamp, key, value, headers, callbacks, dq, nowMs);\\n388:         if (appendResult != null) {\\n389:             // Somebody else found us a batch, return the one we waited for! Hopefully this doesn't happen often...\\n390:             return appendResult;\\n391:         }\\n392: \\n393:         MemoryRecordsBuilder recordsBuilder = recordsBuilder(buffer);\\n394:         ProducerBatch batch = new ProducerBatch(new TopicPartition(topic, partition), recordsBuilder, nowMs);\\n395:         FutureRecordMetadata future = Objects.requireNonNull(batch.tryAppend(timestamp, key, value, headers,\\n396:                 callbacks, nowMs));\\n397: \\n398:         dq.addLast(batch);\\n399:         incomplete.add(batch);\\n400: \\n401:         return new RecordAppendResult(future, dq.size() > 1 || batch.isFull(), true, batch.estimatedSizeInBytes());\\n402:     }\\n403: \\n404:     private MemoryRecordsBuilder recordsBuilder(ByteBuffer buffer) {\\n405:         return MemoryRecords.builder(buffer, RecordBatch.CURRENT_MAGIC_VALUE, compression, TimestampType.CREATE_TIME, 0L);\\n406:     }\\n407: \\n408:     /**\\n409:      * Check if all batches in the queue are full.\\n410:      */\\n411:     private boolean allBatchesFull(Deque<ProducerBatch> deque) {\\n412:         // Only the last batch may be incomplete, so we just check that.\\n413:         ProducerBatch last = deque.peekLast();\\n414:         return last == null || last.isFull();\\n415:     }\\n416: \\n417:      /**\\n418:      *  Try to append to a ProducerBatch.\\n419:      *\\n420:      *  If it is full, we return null and a new batch is created. We also close the batch for record appends to free up\\n421:      *  resources like compression buffers. The batch will be fully closed (ie. the record batch headers will be written\\n422:      *  and memory records built) in one of the following cases (whichever comes first): right before send,\\n423:      *  if it is expired, or when the producer is closed.\\n424:      */\\n425:     private RecordAppendResult tryAppend(long timestamp, byte[] key, byte[] value, Header[] headers,\\n426:                                          Callback callback, Deque<ProducerBatch> deque, long nowMs) {\\n427:         if (closed)\\n428:             throw new KafkaException(\\\"Producer closed while send in progress\\\");\\n429:         ProducerBatch last = deque.peekLast();\\n430:         if (last != null) {\\n431:             int initialBytes = last.estimatedSizeInBytes();\\n432:             FutureRecordMetadata future = last.tryAppend(timestamp, key, value, headers, callback, nowMs);\\n433:             if (future == null) {\\n434:                 last.closeForRecordAppends();\\n435:             } else {\\n436:                 int appendedBytes = last.estimatedSizeInBytes() - initialBytes;\\n437:                 return new RecordAppendResult(future, deque.size() > 1 || last.isFull(), false, appendedBytes);\\n438:             }\\n439:         }\\n440:         return null;\\n441:     }\\n442: \\n443:     private boolean isMuted(TopicPartition tp) {\\n444:         return muted.contains(tp);\\n445:     }\\n446: \\n447:     public void resetNextBatchExpiryTime() {\\n448:         nextBatchExpiryTimeMs = Long.MAX_VALUE;\\n449:     }\\n450: \\n451:     public void maybeUpdateNextBatchExpiryTime(ProducerBatch batch) {\\n452:         if (batch.createdMs + deliveryTimeoutMs  > 0) {\\n453:             // the non-negative check is to guard us against potential overflow due to setting\\n454:             // a large value for deliveryTimeoutMs\\n455:             nextBatchExpiryTimeMs = Math.min(nextBatchExpiryTimeMs, batch.createdMs + deliveryTimeoutMs);\\n456:         } else {\\n457:             log.warn(\\\"Skipping next batch expiry time update due to addition overflow: \\\"\\n458:                 + \\\"batch.createMs={}, deliveryTimeoutMs={}\\\", batch.createdMs, deliveryTimeoutMs);\\n459:         }\\n460:     }\\n461: \\n462:     /**\\n463:      * Get a list of batches which have been sitting in the accumulator too long and need to be expired.\\n464:      */\\n465:     public List<ProducerBatch> expiredBatches(long now) {\\n466:         List<ProducerBatch> expiredBatches = new ArrayList<>();\\n467:         for (TopicInfo topicInfo : topicInfoMap.values()) {\\n468:             for (Deque<ProducerBatch> deque : topicInfo.batches.values()) {\\n469:                 // expire the batches in the order of sending\\n470:                 synchronized (deque) {\\n471:                     while (!deque.isEmpty()) {\\n472:                         ProducerBatch batch = deque.getFirst();\\n473:                         if (batch.hasReachedDeliveryTimeout(deliveryTimeoutMs, now)) {\\n474:                             deque.poll();\\n475:                             batch.abortRecordAppends();\\n476:                             expiredBatches.add(batch);\\n477:                         } else {\\n478:                             maybeUpdateNextBatchExpiryTime(batch);\\n479: In Sender.completeBatch method, we check\\n494:      * whether the batch has reached deliveryTimeoutMs or not. Hence we do not do the delivery timeout check here.\\n495:      */\\n496:     public void reenqueue(ProducerBatch batch, long now) {\\n497:         batch.reenqueued(now);\\n498:         Deque<ProducerBatch> deque = getOrCreateDeque(batch.topicPartition);\\n499:         synchronized (deque) {\\n500:             if (transactionManager != null)\\n501:                 insertInSequenceOrder(deque, batch);\\n502:             else\\n503:                 deque.addFirst(batch);\\n504:         }\\n505:     }\\n506: \\n507:     /**\\n508:      * Split the big batch that has been rejected and reenqueue the split batches in to the accumulator.\\n509:      * @return the number of split batches.\\n510:      */\\n511:     public int splitAndReenqueue(ProducerBatch bigBatch) {\\n512:         // Reset the estimated compression ratio to the initial value or the big batch compression ratio, whichever\\n513:         // is bigger. There are several different ways to do the reset. We chose the most conservative one to ensure\\n514:         // the split doesn't happen too often.\\n515:         CompressionRatioEstimator.setEstimation(bigBatch.topicPartition.topic(), compression.type(),\\n516:                                                 Math.max(1.0f, (float) bigBatch.compressionRatio()));\\n517:         Deque<ProducerBatch> dq = bigBatch.split(this.batchSize);\\n518:         int numSplitBatches = dq.size();\\n519:         Deque<ProducerBatch> partitionDequeue = getOrCreateDeque(bigBatch.topicPartition);\\n520:         while (!dq.isEmpty()) {\\n521:             ProducerBatch batch = dq.pollLast();\\n522:             incomplete.add(batch);\\n523:             // We treat the newly split batches as if they are not even tried.\\n524:             synchronized (partitionDequeue) {\\n525:                 if (transactionManager != null) {\\n526:                     // We should track the newly created batches since they already have assigned sequences.\\n527:                     transactionManager.addInFlightBatch(batch);\\n528:                     insertInSequenceOrder(partitionDequeue, batch);\\n529:                 } else {\\n530:                     partitionDequeue.addFirst(batch);\\n531:                 }\\n532:             }\\n533:         }\\n534:         return numSplitBatches;\\n535:     }\\n536: \\n537:     // We will have to do extra work to ensure the queue is in order when requests are being retried and there are\\n538:     // multiple requests in flight to that partition. If the first in flight request fails to append, then all the\\n539:     // subsequent in flight requests will also fail because the sequence numbers will not be accepted.\\n540:     //\\n541:     // Further, once batches are being retried, we are reduced to a single in flight request for that partition. So when\\n542:     // the subsequent batches come back in sequence order, they will have to be placed further back in the queue.\\n543:     //\\n544:     // Note that this assumes that all the batches in the queue which have an assigned sequence also have the current\\n545:     // producer id. We will not attempt to reorder messages if the producer id has changed, we will throw an\\n546:     // IllegalStateException instead.\\n547:     private void insertInSequenceOrder(Deque<ProducerBatch> deque, ProducerBatch batch) {\\n548:         // When we are re-enqueueing and have enabled idempotence, the re-enqueued batch must always have a sequence.\\n549:         if (batch.baseSequence() == RecordBatch.NO_SEQUENCE)\\n550:             throw new IllegalStateException(\\\"Trying to re-enqueue a batch which doesn't have a sequence even \\\" +\\n551:                 \\\"though idempotency is enabled.\\\");\\n552: \\n553:         if (!transactionManager.hasInflightBatches(batch.topicPartition))\\n554:             throw new IllegalStateException(\\\"We are re-enqueueing a batch which is not tracked as part of the in flight \\\" +\\n555:                 \\\"requests. batch.topicPartition: \\\" + batch.topicPartition + \\\"; batch.baseSequence: \\\" + batch.baseSequence());\\n556: \\n557:         ProducerBatch firstBatchInQueue = deque.peekFirst();\\n558:         if (firstBatchInQueue != null && firstBatchInQueue.hasSequence() && firstBatchInQueue.baseSequence() < batch.baseSequence()) {\\n559:             // The incoming batch can't be inserted at the front of the queue without violating the sequence ordering.\\n560:             // This means that the incoming batch should be placed somewhere further back.\\n561:             // We need to find the right place for the incoming batch and insert it there.\\n562:             // We will only enter this branch if we have multiple inflights sent to different brokers and we need to retry\\n563:             // the inflight batches.\\n564:             //\\n565:             // Since we reenqueue exactly one batch a time and ensure that the queue is ordered by sequence always, it\\n566:             // is a simple linear scan of a subset of the in flight batches to find the right place in the queue each time.\\n567:             List<ProducerBatch> orderedBatches = new ArrayList<>();\\n568:             while (deque.peekFirst() != null && deque.peekFirst().hasSequence() && deque.peekFirst().baseSequence() < batch.baseSequence())\\n569:                 orderedBatches.add(deque.pollFirst());\\n570: \\n571:             log.debug(\\\"Reordered incoming batch with sequence {} for partition {}. It was placed in the queue at \\\" +\\n572:                 \\\"position {}\\\", batch.baseSequence(), batch.topicPartition, orderedBatches.size());\\n573:             // Either we have reached a point where there are batches without a sequence (ie. never been drained\\n574:             // and are hence in order by default), or the batch at the front of the queue has a sequence greater\\n575:             // than the incoming batch. This is the right place to add the incoming batch.\\n576:             deque.addFirst(batch);\\n577: \\n578:             // Now we have to re insert the previously queued batches in the right order.\\n579:             for (int i = orderedBatches.size() - 1; i >= 0; --i) {\\n580:                 deque.addFirst(orderedBatches.get(i));\\n581:             }\\n582: \\n583:             // At this point, the incoming batch has been queued in the correct place according to its sequence.\\n584:         } else {\\n585:             deque.addFirst(batch);\\n586:         }\\n587:     }\\n588: \\n589:     /**\\n590:      * Add the leader to the ready nodes if the batch is ready\\n591:      *\\n592:      * @param exhausted 'true' is the buffer pool is exhausted\\n593:      * @param part The partition\\n594:      * @param leader The leader for the partition\\n595:      * @param waitedTimeMs How long batch waited\\n596:      * @param backingOff Is backing off\\n597:      * @param backoffAttempts Number of attempts for calculating backoff delay\\n598:      * @param full Is batch full\\n599:      * @param nextReadyCheckDelayMs The delay for next check\\n600:      * @param readyNodes The set of ready nodes (to be filled in)\\n601:      * @return The delay for next check\\n602:      */\\n603:     private long batchReady(boolean exhausted, TopicPartition part, Node leader,\\n604:                             long waitedTimeMs, boolean backingOff, int backoffAttempts,\\n605:                             boolean full, long nextReadyCheckDelayMs, Set<Node> readyNodes) {\\n606:         if (!readyNodes.contains(leader) && !isMuted(part)) {\\n607:             long timeToWaitMs = backingOff ? retryBackoff.backoff(backoffAttempts > 0 ? backoffAttempts - 1 : 0) : lingerMs;\\n608:             boolean expired = waitedTimeMs >= timeToWaitMs;\\n609:             boolean transactionCompleting = transactionManager != null && transactionManager.isCompleting();\\n610:             boolean sendable = full\\n611:                     || expired\\n612:                     || exhausted\\n613:                     || closed\\n614:                     || flushInProgress()\\n615:                     || transactionCompleting;\\n616:             if (sendable && !backingOff) {\\n617:                 readyNodes.add(leader);\\n618:             } else {\\n619:                 long timeLeftMs = Math.max(timeToWaitMs - waitedTimeMs, 0);\\n620:                 // Note that this results in a conservative estimate since an un-sendable partition may have\\n621:                 // a leader that will later be found to have sendable data. However, this is good enough\\n622:                 // since we'll just wake up and then sleep again for the remaining time.\\n623:                 nextReadyCheckDelayMs = Math.min(timeLeftMs, nextReadyCheckDelayMs);\\n624:             }\\n625:         }\\n626:         return nextReadyCheckDelayMs;\\n627:     }\\n628: \\n629:     /**\\n630:      * Iterate over partitions to see which one have batches ready and collect leaders of those\\n631:      * partitions into the set of ready nodes. The reason is that we build queue sizes from the batches map,\\n654:             // and if an entry is missing in the batches map, then adaptive partitioning logic\\n655:             // won't know about it and won't switch to it.\\n656:             queueSizes = new int[batches.size()];\\n657:             partitionIds = new int[queueSizes.length];\\n658:         }\\n659: \\n660:         int queueSizesIndex = -1;\\n661:         boolean exhausted = this.free.queued() > 0;\\n662:         for (Map.Entry<Integer, Deque<ProducerBatch>> entry : batches.entrySet()) {\\n663:             TopicPartition part = new TopicPartition(topic, entry.getKey());\\n664:             // Advance queueSizesIndex so that we properly index available\\n665:             // partitions.  Do it here so that it's done for all code paths.\\n666: \\n667:             Node leader = metadataSnapshot.cluster().leaderFor(part);\\n668:             if (leader != null && queueSizes != null) {\\n669:                 ++queueSizesIndex;\\n670:                 assert queueSizesIndex < queueSizes.length;\\n671:                 partitionIds[queueSizesIndex] = part.partition();\\n672:             }\\n673: \\n674:             Deque<ProducerBatch> deque = entry.getValue();\\n675: \\n676:             final long waitedTimeMs;\\n677:             final boolean backingOff;\\n678:             final int backoffAttempts;\\n679:             final int dequeSize;\\n680:             final boolean full;\\n681: \\n682:             OptionalInt leaderEpoch = metadataSnapshot.leaderEpochFor(part);\\n683: \\n684:             // This loop is especially hot with large partition counts. So -\\n685: \\n686:             // 1. We should avoid code that increases synchronization between application thread calling\\n687:             // send(), and background thread running runOnce(), see https://issues.apache.org/jira/browse/KAFKA-16226\\n688: \\n689:             // 2. We are careful to only perform the minimum required inside the\\n690:             // synchronized block, as this lock is also used to synchronize producer threads\\n691:             // attempting to append() to a partition/batch.\\n692: \\n693:             synchronized (deque) {\\n694:                 // Deques are often empty in this path, esp with large partition counts,\\n695:                 // so we exit early if we can.\\n696:                 ProducerBatch batch = deque.peekFirst();\\n697:                 if (batch == null) {\\n698:                     continue;\\n699:                 }\\n700: \\n701:                 waitedTimeMs = batch.waitedTimeMs(nowMs);\\n702:                 batch.maybeUpdateLeaderEpoch(leaderEpoch);\\n703:                 backingOff =           full = dequeSize > 1 || batch.isFull();\\n707:             }\\n708: \\n709:             if (leader == null) {\\n710:                 // This is a partition for which leader is not known, but messages are available to send.\\n711:                 // Note that entries are currently not removed from batches when deque is empty.\\n712:                 unknownLeaderTopics.add(part.topic());\\n713:             } else {\\n714:                 if (queueSizes != null)\\n715:                     queueSizes[queueSizesIndex] = dequeSize;\\n716:                 if (partitionAvailabilityTimeoutMs > 0) {\\n717:                     // Check if we want to exclude the partition from the list of available partitions\\n718:                     // if the broker hasn't responded for some time.\\n719:                     NodeLatencyStats nodeLatencyStats = nodeStats.get(leader.id());\\n720:                     if (nodeLatencyStats != null) {\\n721:                         // NOTE: there is no synchronization between reading metrics,\\n722:                         // so we read ready time first to avoid accidentally marking partition\\n723:                         // unavailable if we read while the metrics are being updated.\\n724:                         long readyTimeMs = nodeLatencyStats.readyTimeMs;\\n725:                         if (readyTimeMs - nodeLatencyStats.drainTimeMs > partitionAvailabilityTimeoutMs)\\n726:                             --queueSizesIndex;\\n727:                     }\\n728:                 }\\n729: \\n730:                 nextReadyCheckDelayMs = batchReady(exhausted, part, leader, waitedTimeMs, backingOff,\\n731:                     backoffAttempts, full, nextReadyCheckDelayMs, readyNodes);\\n732:             }\\n733:         }\\n734: \\n735:         // We've collected the queue sizes for partitions of this topic, now we can calculate\\n736:         // load stats. queueSizesIndex + 1);\\n739:         return nextReadyCheckDelayMs;\\n740:     }\\n741: \\n742:     /**\\n743:      * Get a list of nodes whose partitions are ready to be sent, and the earliest time at which any non-sendable\\n744:      * partition will be ready; Also return the flag for whether there are any unknown leaders for the accumulated\\n745:      * partition batches.\\n746:      * <p>\\n747:      * A destination node is ready to send data if:\\n748:      * <ol>\\n749:      * <li>There is at least one partition that is not backing off its send\\n750:      * <li><b>and</b> those partitions are not muted (to prevent reordering if\\n751:      *   {@value org.apache.kafka.clients.producer.ProducerConfig#MAX_IN_FLIGHT_REQUESTS_PER_CONNECTION}\\n752:      *   is set to one)</li>\\n753:      * <li><b>and <i>any</i></b> of the following are true</li>\\n754:      * <ul>\\n755:      *     <li>The record set is full</li>\\n756:      *     <li>The record set has sat in the accumulator for at least lingerMs milliseconds</li>\\n757:      *     <li>The accumulator is out of memory and threads are blocking waiting for data (in this case all partitions\\n758:      *     are immediately considered ready).</li>\\n759:      *     <li>The accumulator has been closed</li>\\n760:      * </ul>\\n761:      * </ol>\\n762:      */\\n763:     public ReadyCheckResult ready(MetadataSnapshot metadataSnapshot, long nowMs) {\\n764:         Set<Node> readyNodes = new HashSet<>();\\n765:         long nextReadyCheckDelayMs = Long.MAX_VALUE;\\n766:         Set<String> unknownLeaderTopics = new HashSet<>();\\n767:         // Go topic by topic so that we can get queue sizes for partitions in a topic and calculate\\n768:         // cumulative frequency table (used in partitioner).\\n769:         for (Map.Entry<String, TopicInfo> topicInfoEntry : this.topicInfoMap.entrySet()) {\\n770:             final String topic = topicInfoEntry.getKey();\\n771:             nextReadyCheckDelayMs = partitionReady(metadataSnapshot, nowMs, topic, topicInfoEntry.getValue(), nextReadyCheckDelayMs, readyNodes, unknownLeaderTopics);\\n772:         }\\n773:         return new ReadyCheckResult(readyNodes, nextReadyCheckDelayMs, unknownLeaderTopics);\\n774:     }\\n775: \\n776:     /**\\n777:      * Check whether there are any batches which haven't been drained\\n778:      */\\n779:     public boolean hasUndrained() {\\n780:         for (TopicInfo topicInfo : topicInfoMap.values()) {\\n781:             for (Deque<ProducerBatch> deque : topicInfo.batches.values()) {\\n782:                 synchronized (deque) {\\n783:                     if (!deque.isEmpty())\\n784:                         return true;\\n785:                 }\\n786:             }\\n787:         }\\n788:         return false;\\n789:     }\\n790: \\n791:     private boolean shouldBackoff(boolean hasLeaderChanged, final ProducerBatch batch, final long waitedTimeMs) {\\n792:         boolean shouldWaitMore = batch.attempts() > 0 && waitedTimeMs < retryBackoff.backoff(batch.attempts() - 1);\\n793:         boolean shouldBackoff = !hasLeaderChanged && shouldWaitMore;\\n794:         if (log.isTraceEnabled()) {\\n795:             if (shouldBackoff) {\\n796:                 log.trace(\\n797:                     \\\"For {}, will backoff\\\", batch);\\n798:             } else {\\n799:                 log.trace(\\n800:                     \\\"For {}, will not backoff, shouldWaitMore {}, hasLeaderChanged {}\\\", batch,\\n801:                     shouldWaitMore, hasLeaderChanged);\\n802:             }\\n803:         } else if (log.isDebugEnabled() && hasLeaderChanged) {\\n804:             // Add less-verbose log at DEBUG.\\n805:             log.debug(\\\"For {}, leader has changed, hence skipping backoff.\\\", batch);\\n806:         }\\n807:         return shouldBackoff;\\n808:     }\\n809: \\n810:     private boolean shouldStopDrainBatchesForPartition(ProducerBatch first, TopicPartition tp) {\\n811:         ProducerIdAndEpoch producerIdAndEpoch;\\n812:         if (transactionManager != null) {\\n813:             if (!transactionManager.isSendToPartitionAllowed(tp))\\n814:                 return true;\\n815: \\n816:             producerIdAndEpoch = transactionManager.producerIdAndEpoch();\\n817:             if (!producerIdAndEpoch.isValid())\\n818:                 // we cannot send the batch until we have refreshed the producer id\\n819:                 return true;\\n820: \\n821:             if (!first.hasSequence()) {\\n822:                 if (transactionManager.hasInflightBatches(tp) && transactionManager.hasStaleProducerIdAndEpoch(tp)) {\\n823:                     // Don't drain any new batches while the partition has in-flight batches with a different epoch\\n824:                     // and/or producer ID. Otherwise, a batch with a new epoch and sequence number\\n825:                     // 0 could be written before earlier batches complete, which would cause out of sequence errors\\n826:                     return true;\\n827:                 }\\n828: \\n829:                 if (transactionManager.hasUnresolvedSequence(first.topicPartition))\\n830:                     // Don't drain any new batches while the state of previous sequence numbers\\n831:                     // is unknown. The previous batches would be unknown if they were aborted\\n832:                     // on the client after being sent to the broker at least once.\\n833:                     return true;\\n834:             }\\n835: \\n836:             int firstInFlightSequence = transactionManager.firstInFlightSequence(first.topicPartition);\\n837:             // If the queued batch already has an assigned sequence, then it is being retried.\\n838:             // In this case, we wait until the next immediate batch is ready and drain that.\\n839:             // We only move on when the next in line batch is complete (either successfully or due to\\n840:             // a fatal broker error). This effectively reduces our in flight request count to 1.\\n841:             return firstInFlightSequence != RecordBatch.NO_SEQUENCE && first.hasSequence()\\n842:                     && first.baseSequence() != firstInFlightSequence;\\n843:         }\\n844:         return false;\\n845:     }\\n846: \\n847:     private List<ProducerBatch> drainBatchesForOneNode(MetadataSnapshot
